(function () {
DataHandler.add(new VueConfig({
config: {"tournamentId": 149, "phaseId":107903, "year":2023},
dataUrls: {"dataUrl-0":"https:\/\/hbldata.fmp.sportradar.com\/feeds\/de\/Europe:Berlin\/gismo\/fixtures\/[tournamentId]\/[phaseId]"},
domSelector: '#schedule2164892',
postRenderingFunction: function () {
$('#schedule2164892 table').addClass('footable');
initFootable();
window.setTimeout(function() {
let currentMatchdays = document.querySelectorAll("[data-status=true]");
let currentMatchday = [].slice.call(currentMatchdays).pop();
let scrollToY = currentMatchday.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset - 200;
window.scrollTo( { top: scrollToY, behavior: 'smooth' } );
}, 500);
},
prepareDataFunction: function (data, self) {
var allMatchesByMatchday = { "matchdays": { } };
$.each(data[0]['doc'][0]['data']['tournament']['phases'][0]['matchdays'], function (index, matchday) {
var matchdayNumber = matchday['round_number'];
if (typeof allMatchesByMatchday["matchdays"][matchdayNumber] === 'undefined') {
allMatchesByMatchday["matchdays"][matchdayNumber] = {
"round_number": matchdayNumber,
"current": matchday['current_matchday'],
"matchStatus": {
"confirmed_result": { "matches": [] },
"in_progress": { "matches": [] },
"scheduled": { "matches": [] }
}
};
}
$.each(matchday.matches, function (index, match) {
var matchStatus = match["status"];
if (matchStatus == 'postponed' || matchStatus == 'scheduled_unknown_date' || matchStatus == 'scheduled_unknown_time') {
allMatchesByMatchday["matchdays"][matchdayNumber]['matchStatus']["scheduled"]["matches"].push(match);
} else if (matchStatus == 'played' || matchStatus == 'confirmed_by_scout' || matchStatus == 'abandoned' || matchStatus == 'forfeit') {
allMatchesByMatchday["matchdays"][matchdayNumber]['matchStatus']["confirmed_result"]["matches"].push(match);
} else {
allMatchesByMatchday["matchdays"][matchdayNumber]['matchStatus'][matchStatus]["matches"].push(match);
}
});
allMatchesByMatchday["matchdays"][matchdayNumber]['matchStatus']["confirmed_result"]["matches"].sort(function (a, b) {
return parseFloat(a.play_date.uts) - parseFloat(b.play_date.uts);
});
allMatchesByMatchday["matchdays"][matchdayNumber]['matchStatus']["in_progress"]["matches"].sort(function (a, b) {
return parseFloat(a.play_date.uts) - parseFloat(b.play_date.uts);
});
allMatchesByMatchday["matchdays"][matchdayNumber]['matchStatus']["scheduled"]["matches"].sort(function (a, b) {
return parseFloat(a.play_date.uts) - parseFloat(b.play_date.uts);
});
});
return allMatchesByMatchday;
}
}));
}());
